<Rung Number="25" Type="N">
<Comment>
<![CDATA[every sensor must be free
Steps:
Start from touchpanel button. It is at the manual feeder page.
10=Start run to reference positioning sequense
  -> 1=Manual or automatic no connected
  -> 2=reserve
11=Run backward
  -> 3=Time_Out (reference sensor not found)
12= At the reference sensor and after that Run slowly forward
13=Reference position is set
]]>
</Comment>
